selecting the syntax, see <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="919878012" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/issues/1687" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/sharkdp/bat/pull/1687/hovercard" href="https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/pull/1687">#1687</a> (<a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/scop/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/scop">@scop</a>)</li> </ul> <h2>Bugfixes</h2> <ul> <li>Fix for a security vulnerability on Windows (<a href="https://cve.mitre.org/cgi-bin/cvename.cgi?name=CVE-2021-36753" rel="nofollow">CVE-2021-36753</a>). Prior to this release, <code>bat</code> would execute programs called <code>less</code>/<code>less.exe</code> from the current working directory (instead of the one from <code>PATH</code>) with priority. An attacker might be able to use this by placing a malicious program in a shared directory where the user would execute <code>bat</code>. <code>bat</code> users on Windows are advised to upgrade to this version. See <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="942313623" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/issues/1724" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="777592373" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/issues/1472" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/sharkdp/bat/issues/1472/hovercard" href="https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/issues/1472">#1472</a> (<a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/Ry0taK/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/Ry0taK">@Ry0taK</a>).</li> </ul> <h2>Other</h2> <ul>
